64**](#chapter_64) [**Chapter 65**](#chapter_65) [**Chapter 66**](#chapter_66) **Chapter 1** [(Top)](#top) ***      The vision of Isaiah, the son of Amoz, which he saw concerning Judah and Jerusalem during the days of Uzziah, Jotham, Ahaz, and Hezekiah—kings of Judah. (1:1) -Parry      The vision of Isaiah the son of Amoz, which he saw concerning Judah and Jerusalem in the days of Uzziah, Jotham, Ahaz, and Hezekiah, kings of Judah. (1:1) -KJV      The vision concerning Judah and Jerusalem that Isaiah son of Amoz saw during the reigns of Uzziah, Jotham, Ahaz and Hezekiah, kings of Judah. (1:1) -NIV      The vision of Isaiah the son of Amoz which he beheld concerning Judea and Jerusalem during the reigns of Uzziah, Jotham, Ahaz, and Hezekiah, kings of Judah: (1:1) -Gileadi      Hear, O heavens, and listen, O earth; for the LORD has spoken:I have reared and raised children, but they rebelled against me. (1:2) -Parry      Hear, O heavens, and give ear, O earth: for the Lord hath spoken, I have nourished and brought up children, and they have rebelled against me. (1:2) -KJV      Hear, O heavens! Listen, O earth! For the LORD has spoken: “I reared children and brought them up, but they have rebelled against me. (1:2) -NIV      Hear, O heavens! Give heed, O earth! Jehovah has spoken: I have reared sons, brought them up, but they have revolted against me. (1:2) -Gileadi      The ox knows its purchaser and the ass its owner's feeding trough; Israel does not know, my people do not understand. (1:3) -Parry      The ox knoweth his owner, and the ass his master's crib: but Israel doth not know, my people doth not consider. (1:3) -KJV      The ox knows his master, the donkey his owner’s manger, but Israel does not know, my people do not understand.” (1:3) -NIV      The ox knows its owner, the ass its master’s stall, but Israel does not know; my people are insensible. (1:3) -Gileadi      Woe, nation that sins, people burdened with iniquity, seed of evildoers, children who are corrupt. They have abandoned the LORD; they have spurned the Holy One of Israel; they have turned their backs. (1:4) -Parry      Ah sinful nation, a people laden with iniquity, a seed of evildoers, children that are corrupters: they have forsaken the Lord, they have provoked the Holy One of Israel unto anger, they are gone away backward. (1:4) -KJV      Ah, sinful nation, a people loaded with guilt, a brood of evildoers, children given to corruption! They have forsaken the LORD ; they have spurned the Holy One of Israel and turned their backs on him. (1:4) -NIV      Alas, a nation astray, a people weighed down by sin, the offspring of wrongdoers, perverse children: they have forsaken Jehovah, they have spurned the Holy One of Israel, they have lapsed into apostasy. (1:4) -Gileadi      Why will you be smitten again? You continuously revolt. Your entire head is sick; your entire heart is diseased. (1:5) -Parry      Why should ye be stricken any more? ye will revolt more and more: the whole head is sick, and the whole heart faint. (1:5) -KJV      Why should you be beaten anymore? Why do you persist in rebellion? Your whole head is injured, your whole heart afflicted. (1:5) -NIV      Why be smitten further by adding to your waywardness? The whole head is sick, the whole heart diseased. (1:5) -Gileadi      From the sole of the foot to the head, there is no healthy spot. Wounds, and bruises, and open sores—they have not been closed up nor wrapped, neither softened with ointment. (1:6) -Parry      From the sole of the foot even unto the head there is no soundness in it; but wounds, and bruises, and putrifying sores: they have not been closed, neither bound up, neither mollified with ointment. (1:6) -KJV      From the sole of your foot to the top of your head there is no soundness— only wounds and welts and open sores, not cleansed or bandaged or soothed with oil. (1:6) -NIV      From the soles of the feet even to the head there is nothing sound, only wounds and bruises and festering sores; they have not been pressed out or bound up, nor soothed with ointment. (1:6) -Gileadi      Your land is desolate, your cities are burned with fire, your soil, strangers devour in your presence, it is desolate, overthrown by strangers. (1:7) -Parry      Your country is desolate, your cities are burned with fire: your land, strangers devour it in your presence, and it is desolate, as over thrown by strangers. (1:7) -KJV      Your country is desolate, your cities burned with fire; your fields are being stripped by foreigners right before you, laid waste as when overthrown by strangers. (1:7) -NIV      Your land is ruined, your cities burned with fire; your native soil is devoured by aliens in your presence, laid waste at its takeover by foreigners. (1:7) -Gileadi      And the daughter of Zion is left as a hut in a vineyard, as a shelter in a cucumber field, as a besieged city. (1:8) -Parry      And the daughter of Zion is left as a cottage in a vineyard, as a lodge in a garden of cucumbers, as a be sieged city. (1:8) -KJV      The Daughter of Zion is left like a shelter in a vineyard, like a hut in a field of melons, like a city under siege. (1:8) -NIV      The Daughter of Zion is left like a shelter in a vineyard, a hut in a melon field, a city under siege. (1:8) -Gileadi      If the LORD of Hosts had not left us a few survivors, we would be like Sodom, we would be as Gomorrah. (1:9) -Parry      Except the Lord of hosts had left unto us a very small remnant, we should have been as Sodom, and we should have been like unto Gomorrah. (1:9) -KJV      Unless the LORD Almighty had left us some survivors, we would have become like Sodom, we would have been like Gomorrah. (1:9) -NIV      Had not Jehovah of Hosts left us a few survivors, we should have been as Sodom, or become like Gomorrah. (1:9) -Gileadi      Hear the word of the LORD, rulers of Sodom; listen to the law of our God, people of Gomorrah. (1:10) -Parry      Hear the word of the Lord, ye rulers of Sodom; give ear unto the law of our God, ye people of Gomorrah. (1:10) -KJV      Hear the word of the LORD, you rulers of Sodom; listen to the law of our God, you people of Gomorrah! (1:10) -NIV      Hear the word of Jehovah, O leaders of Sodom; give heed to the law of our God, you people of Gomorrah! (1:10) -Gileadi      What is the multitude of your sacrifices to me? says the LORD. I have had enough of burnt offerings of rams, and the fat of fattened beasts and the blood of bulls. I do not delight in lambs or he-goats. (1:11) -Parry      To what purpose is the multitude of your sacrifices unto me? saith the Lord: I am full of the burnt offerings of rams, and the fat of fed beasts; and I delight not in the blood of bullocks, or of lambs, or of he goats. (1:11) -KJV      “The multitude of your sacrifices— what are they to me?” says the LORD. “I have more than enough of burnt offerings, of rams and the fat of fattened animals; I have no pleasure in the blood of bulls and lambs and goats. (1:11) -NIV      For what purpose are your abundant sacrifices to me? says Jehovah. I have had my fill of offerings of rams and fat of fatted beasts; the blood of bulls and sheep and he-goats I do not want. (1:11) -Gileadi      When you come to see my face, who requires this from your hand to trample my courts? (1:12) -Parry      When ye come to appear before me, who hath required this at your hand, to tread my courts? (1:12) -KJV      When you come to appear before me, who has asked this of you, this trampling of my courts? (1:12) -NIV      When you come to see me, who requires you to trample my courts so? (1:12) -Gileadi      Bring no more meaningless offerings; incense is an abomination unto me; the new moons and sabbaths, the calling of assemblies—I cannot endure iniquity and the solemn assembly; (1:13) -Parry      Bring no more vain oblations; incense is an abomination unto me; the new moons and sabbaths, the calling of assemblies, I cannot away with;it is iniquity, even the solemn meeting. (1:13) -KJV      Stop bringing meaningless offerings! Your incense is detestable to me. New Moons, Sabbaths and convocations— I cannot bear your evil assemblies. (1:13) -NIV      Bring no more worthless offerings; they are as a loathsome incense to me. As for convening meetings at the New Month and on the Sabbath, wickedness with the solemn gathering I cannot approve. (1:13) -Gileadi      my soul hates your new moons and your appointed feasts; they have become a burden to me; I am weary of bearing them. (1:14) -Parry      Your new moons and your appointed feasts my soul hateth: they are a trouble unto me; I am weary to bear them. (1:14) -KJV      Your New Moon festivals and your appointed feasts my soul hates. They have become a burden to me; I am weary of bearing them. (1:14) -NIV      Your monthly and regular meetings my soul detests. They have become a burden on me; I am weary of putting up with them. (1:14) -Gileadi      And when you spread forth your palms, I will hide mine eyes from you; even when you pray much, I will not hear. Your hands are full of blood, [your fingers with iniquity]. (1:15) -Parry      And when ye spread forth your hands, I will hide mine eyes from you: yea, when ye make many prayers, I will not hear: your hands are full of blood. (1:15) -KJV      When you spread out your hands in prayer, I will hide my eyes from you; even if you offer many prayers, I will not listen. Your hands are full of blood; (1:15) -NIV      When you spread forth your hands, I will conceal my eyes from you; though you pray at length, I will not hear— your hands are filled with blood. (1:15) -Gileadi      Wash yourselves. Be pure. Remove the evil of your deeds from before my eyes. Stop the evil. (1:16) -Parry      Wash you, make you clean; put away the evil of your doings from before mine eyes; cease to do evil; (1:16) -KJV      wash and make yourselves clean. Take your evil deeds out of my sight! Stop doing wrong, (1:16) -NIV      Wash yourselves clean: remove your wicked deeds from before my eyes; cease to do evil. (1:16) -Gileadi      Learn to do well; seek justice, relieve the oppressed, defend the orphan, plead for the widow. (1:17) -Parry      Learn to do well; seek judgment, relieve the oppressed, judge the fatherless, plead for the widow. (1:17) -KJV      learn to do right! Seek justice, encourage the oppressed. (Or rebuke the oppressor) Defend the cause of the fatherless, plead the case of the widow. (1:17) -NIV      Learn to do good: demand justice, stand up for the oppressed; plead the cause of the fatherless, appeal on behalf of the widow. (1:17) -Gileadi      Come and let us reason together, says the LORD:Though your sins are as scarlet, they will be as white as snow; though they are red like crimson, they will be as wool. (1:18) -Parry      Come now, and let us reason together, saith the Lord: though your sins be as scarlet, they shall be as white as snow; though they be red like crimson, they shall be as wool. (1:18) -KJV      “Come now, let us reason together,” says the LORD. “Though your sins are like scarlet, they shall be as white as snow; though they are red as crimson, they shall be like wool. (1:18) -NIV      Come now, let us put it to the test, says Jehovah: though your sins are as scarlet, they can be made white as snow; though they have reddened as crimson, they may become white as wool. (1:18) -Gileadi      If you are willing and obedient, you will eat the good of the land; (1:19) -Parry      If ye be willing and obedient, ye shall eat the good of the land: (1:19) -KJV      If you are willing and obedient, you will eat the best from the land; (1:19) -NIV      If you are willing and obey, you shall eat the good of the land. (1:19) -Gileadi      but if you refuse and rebel, you will be consumed by the sword, for the mouth of the LORD has spoken. (1:20) -Parry      But if ye refuse and rebel, ye shall be devoured with the sword: for the mouth of the Lord hath spoken it. (1:20) -KJV      but if you resist and rebel, you will be devoured by the sword.” For the mouth of the LORD has spoken. (1:20) -NIV      But if you are unwilling and disobey, you shall be eaten by the sword. By his mouth Jehovah has spoken it. (1:20) -Gileadi      How the faithful city has become a harlot! It was full of justice; righteousness lodged in her, but now murderers. (1:21) -Parry      How is the faithful city become an harlot! it was full of judgment; righteousness lodged in it; but now murderers. (1:21) -KJV      See how the faithful city has become a harlot! She once was full of justice; righteousness used to dwell in her— but now murderers! (1:21) -NIV      How the faithful city has become a harlot! She was filled with justice; righteousness made its abode in her, but now murderers. (1:21) -Gileadi      Your silver has become dross, your wine mixed with water. (1:22) -Parry      Thy silver is become dross, thy wine mixed with water: (1:22) -KJV      Your silver has become dross, your choice wine is diluted with water. (1:22) -NIV      Your silver has become dross, your wine diluted with water. (1:22) -Gileadi      Your rulers are rebels and companions of thieves. [They all] love bribes and chase after gifts. They do not defend the cause of the orphan, neither does the cause of the widow come to them. (1:23) -Parry      Thy princes are rebellious, and companions of thieves: every one loveth gifts, and followeth after rewards: they judge not the fatherless, neither doth the cause of the widow come unto them. (1:23) -KJV      Your rulers are rebels, companions of thieves; they all love bribes and chase after gifts. They do not defend the cause of the fatherless; the widow’s case does not come before them. (1:23) -NIV      Your rulers are renegades, accomplices of robbers: with one accord they love bribes and run after rewards; they do not dispense justice to the fatherless, nor does the widow’s case come before them. (1:23) -Gileadi      Therefore the Lord, the LORD of Hosts, the Mighty One of Israel, speaks:Ah, I will get relief from my adversaries, and avenge myself of mine enemies. (1:24) -Parry      Therefore saith the Lord, the Lord of hosts, the mighty One of Israel, Ah, I will ease me of mine adversaries, and avenge me of mine enemies: (1:24) -KJV      Therefore the Lord, the LORD Almighty, the Mighty One of Israel, declares: “Ah, I will get relief from my foes and avenge myself on my enemies. (1:24) -NIV      Therefore my Lord, Jehovah of Hosts, the Valiant One of Israel, declares, Woe to them! I will relieve me of my adversaries, avenge me of my enemies. (1:24) -Gileadi      And I will turn my hand against you and smelt away your dross and take away all your slag. (1:25) -Parry       And I will turn my hand upon thee, and purely purge away thy dross, and take away all thy tin: (1:25) -KJV      I will turn my hand against you; I will thoroughly purge away your dross and remove all your impurities. (1:25) -NIV      I will restore my hand over you and smelt away your dross as in a crucible (Hebrew kabbor, as with potash/lye, emended to kakur; compare 48:10. ), and remove all your alloy. (1:25) -Gileadi      And I will restore your judges as at the first, and your counselors as at the beginning. Afterward you will be called the City of Righteousness, the Faithful City. (1:26) -Parry      And I will restore thy judges as at the first, and thy counsellors as at the beginning: afterward thou shalt be called, The city of righteousness, the faithful city. (1:26) -KJV      I will restore your judges as in days of old, your counselors as at the beginning. Afterward you will be called the City of Righteousness, the Faithful City.” (1:26) -NIV      I will restore your judges as at the first, and your counselors as in the beginning. After this you shall be called the City of Righteousness, a faithful city. (1:26) -Gileadi      Zion will be redeemed with justice and her repentant ones with righteousness. (1:27) -Parry      Zion shall be redeemed with judgment, and her converts with righteousness. (1:27) -KJV      Zion will be redeemed with justice, her penitent ones with righteousness. (1:27) -NIV      For Zion shall be ransomed by justice, those of her who repent by righteousness. (1:27) -Gileadi      But transgressors and sinners together will be crushed and those that forsake the LORD will be consumed. (1:28) -Parry      And the destruction of the transgressors and of the sinners shall be together, and they that forsake the Lord shall be consumed. (1:28) -KJV      But rebels and sinners will both be broken, and those who forsake the LORD will perish. (1:28) -NIV      But criminals and sinners shall be altogether shattered when those who forsake Jehovah are annihilated. (1:28) -Gileadi      For [you] will be ashamed of the oaks which you have desired, and you will be confounded because of the gardens that you have chosen. (1:29) -Parry      For they shall be ashamed of the oaks which ye have desired, and ye shall be confounded for the gardens that ye have chosen. (1:29) -KJV      “You will be ashamed because of the sacred oaks in which you have delighted; you will be disgraced because of the gardens that you have chosen. (1:29) -NIV      And you will be ashamed of the oaks you cherished and blush for the parks you were fond of; (1:29) -Gileadi      For you will be as an oak whose leaf withers, and as a garden without water. (1:30) -Parry      For ye shall be as an oak whose leaf fadeth, and as a garden that hath no water. (1:30) -KJV      You will be like an oak with fading leaves, like a garden without water. (1:30) -NIV      you shall become like an oak whose leaves wither, and as a garden that has no water. (1:30) -Gileadi      And the strong one will be as tinder, and his work as a spark, and both will burn together, and none will quench them. (1:31) -Parry      And the strong shall be as tow, and the maker of it as a spark, and they shall both burn together, and none shall quench them. (1:31) -KJV      The mighty man will become tinder and his work a spark; both will burn together, with no one to quench the fire.” (1:31) -NIV      The mighty shall be as refuse, and their works a spark; both shall burn up alike, and there shall be none to extinguish. (1:31) -Gileadi *** **Chapter 2** [(Top)](#top) ***      The word that Isaiah, the son of Amoz, saw concerning Judah and Jerusalem. (2:1) -Parry      The word that Isaiah the son of Amoz saw concerning Judah and Jerusalem. (2:1) -KJV      This is what Isaiah son of Amoz saw concerning Judah and Jerusalem: (2:1) -NIV      A prophecy concerning Judea and Jerusalem which Isaiah the son of Amoz saw in vision: (2:1) -Gileadi      And it will come to pass in the last days, [when] the mountain of the LORD's house will be established at the top of the mountains, and it will be exalted above the hills, and all nations will flow unto it. (2:2) -Parry      And it shall come to pass in the last days, that the mountain of the Lord's house shall be established in the top of the mountains, and shall be exalted above the hills; and all nations shall flow unto it. (2:2) -KJV      In the last days the mountain of the LORD's temple will be established as chief among the mountains; it will be raised above the hills, and all nations will stream to it. (2:2) -NIV      In the latter days the mountain of Jehovah’s house shall become established as (So 1QIsaa; MT has bet essentiae: in/as.) the head of the mountains; it shall be preeminent among the hills, and all nations will flow to it. (2:2) -Gileadi      And many people will come and say, Come, and let us go up to the mountain of the LORD to the house of the God of Jacob; that he may teach us of his ways, and that we may walk in his paths; because the law will go forth from Zion, and the word of the LORD from Jerusalem. (2:3) -Parry      And many people shall go and say, Come ye, and let us go up to the mountain of the Lord, to the house of the God of Jacob; and he will teach us of his ways, and we will walk in his paths: for out of Zion shall go forth the law, and the word of the Lord from Jerusalem. (2:3) -KJV      Many peoples will come and say, “Come, let us go up to the mountain of the LORD, to the house of the God of Jacob. He will teach us his ways, so that we may walk in his paths.” The law will go out from Zion, the word of the LORD from Jerusalem. (2:3) -NIV      Many peoples shall go, saying, Come, let us go up to the mountain of Jehovah, to the house of the God of Jacob, that he may instruct us in his ways, that we may follow in his paths. For out of Zion shall go forth the law, and from Jerusalem the word of Jehovah. (2:3) -Gileadi      Thus he will judge among the nations, and he will settle the case for many people. And they will hammer their swords into plowshares, and their spears into pruning hooks. And nation will not lift up a sword against nation, nor will they learn war again. (2:4) -Parry      And he shall judge among the nations, and shall rebuke many people: and they shall beat their swords into plowshares, and their spears into pruning hooks: nation shall not lift up sword against nation, neither shall they learn war any more. (2:4) -KJV      He will judge between the nations and will settle disputes for many peoples. They will beat their swords into plowshares and their spears into pruning hooks. Nation will not take up sword against nation, nor will they train for war anymore. (2:4) -NIV      He will judge between the nations and arbitrate for many peoples. They will beat their swords into plowshares, their spears into pruning hooks: nation will not lift the sword against nation, nor will they learn warfare any more. (2:4) -Gileadi      Come, O house of Jacob, and let us walk in the light of the LORD; [yea, come, for you have all gone astray, every one to his wicked ways]. (2:5) -Parry      O house of Jacob, come ye, and let us walk in the light of the Lord. (2:5) -KJV      Come, O house of Jacob, let us walk in the light of the LORD. (2:5) -NIV      O house of Jacob, come, let us follow the light of Jehovah. (2:5) -Gileadi      Therefore, [O Lord], you have rejected your people, the house of Jacob, because they are filled from the east, and [hearken unto] soothsayers as do the Philistines, and they clasp hands with foreigners. (2:6) -Parry       Therefore thou hast forsaken thy people the house of Jacob, because they be replenished from the east, and are soothsayers like the Philistines, and they please themselves in the children of strangers. (2:6) -KJV      You have abandoned your people, the house of Jacob. They are full of superstitions from the East; they practice divination like the Philistines and clasp hands with pagans. (2:6) -NIV      For you, O Jehovah, have forsaken your people, the house of Jacob, because, like the Philistines, they provide themselves with (Hebrew conjunctive we emended to preposition be.) mystics from the East and are content with the infantile heathen. (2:6) -Gileadi      Their land is full of silver and gold, and there is no end to their treasures. Their land is full of horses and there is no end to their chariots. (2:7) -Parry      Their land also is full of silver and gold, neither is there any end of their treasures; their land is also full of horses, neither is there any end of their chariots: (2:7) -KJV      Their land is full of silver and gold; there is no end to their treasures. Their land is full of horses; there is no end to their chariots. (2:7) -NIV      Their land is full of silver and gold and there is no end to their wealth; their land is full of horses and there is no end to their chariots. (2:7) -Gileadi      Their land is full of idols; they bow down to the work of their hands, that which their fingers have made. (2:8) -Parry      Their land also is full of idols; they worship the work of their own hands, that which their own fingers have made: (2:8) -KJV      Their land is full of idols; they bow down to the work of their hands, to what their fingers have made. (2:8) -NIV      Their land is full of idols: they adore the works of their hands, things their own fingers have made. (2:8) -Gileadi      And mankind has [not] been humbled and man has [not] been brought down; do not forgive them. (2:9) -Parry      And the mean man boweth down, and the great man humbleth himself: therefore forgive them not. (2:9) -KJV      So man will be brought low and mankind humbled— do not forgive them (Or not raise them up). (2:9) -NIV      Mankind is brought low when men thus debase themselves. Forbear them not! (2:9) -Gileadi      [O you wicked ones], enter into the rock, and hide in the dust; for the fear of the LORD and [the glory of] his majesty [will smite you]. (2:10) -Parry       Enter into the rock, and hide thee in the dust, for fear of the Lord, and for the glory of his majesty.
